---
layout: "post"
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus In Agda"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code was tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed in the seminar of logic at Universidad EAFIT.

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

Syntax using indexes.

      <a id="3189" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3191" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3109" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1508" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3199" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3098" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3202" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3204" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3100" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3205" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3102" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2447" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3100" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4291" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5913" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5916" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5918" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2617" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5906" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5928" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5930" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5932" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5933" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5935" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1338" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5941" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5947" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="5982" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5984" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="5988" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4434" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="5992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5992" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="5994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4434" class="Function">]</a> <a id="5996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5916" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1484" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="6005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5933" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="6009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5992" class="Bound">t</a><a id="6010" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6704" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5292" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6678" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6741" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6746" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6748" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6753" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6776" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6778" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6753" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6798" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6803" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6805" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6810" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6811" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6813" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6816" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6821" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6830" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6562" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6810" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7063" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7073" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7075" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7077" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7078" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7079" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7085" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7088" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7090" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2617" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7078" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7100" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7106" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7108" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7109" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1463" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7119" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7125" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7127" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4434" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7135" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4434" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7140" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7088" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7109" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7135" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7151" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7157" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8683" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8764" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8770" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8773" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1463" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8783" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8787" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8788" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8790" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8792" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7063" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8804" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8807" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8773" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8808" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8811" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2392" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8818" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8764" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8828" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8830" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8831" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8832" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8834" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8836" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8842" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8843" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8831" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8854" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10485" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10551" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9954" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9954" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9888" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10568" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10575" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10591" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10593" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9477" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10606" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10608" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9477" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10621" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9477" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10635" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10669" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10702" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10734" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10822" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10870" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
